q0#####SELECT chn.name,t.title   FROM   cast_info AS ci, char_name AS chn, company_name AS cn, company_type AS ct, movie_companies AS mc, role_type AS rt, title AS t  WHERE chn.id = ci.person_role_id AND ci.movie_id = mc.movie_id AND cn.id = mc.company_id AND ct.id = mc.company_type_id AND rt.id = ci.role_id AND t.id = ci.movie_id AND t.id = mc.movie_id AND ((ci.note)::text ~~ '%r%'::text) AND ((cn.country_code)::text = '[suhh]'::text) AND (t.production_year > 1974);
q1#####SELECT cn.name,mi_idx.info,t.title   FROM   company_name AS cn, company_type AS ct, info_type AS it1, info_type AS it2, movie_companies AS mc, movie_info AS mi, movie_info_idx AS mi_idx, title AS t  WHERE cn.id = mc.company_id AND ct.id = mc.company_type_id AND mc.movie_id = mi.movie_id AND mc.movie_id = mi_idx.movie_id AND mi.info_type_id = it1.id AND mi.movie_id = mi_idx.movie_id AND mi_idx.info_type_id = it2.id AND t.id = mc.movie_id AND t.id = mi.movie_id AND t.id = mi_idx.movie_id AND ((cn.country_code)::text = '[eg]'::text) AND ((ct.kind)::text = 'production companies'::text) AND ((it1.info)::text = 'admissions'::text) AND ((mi_idx.info)::text > '10'::text) AND (t.production_year >= 1916) AND (t.production_year <= 2009);
q2#####SELECT mi.info,mi_idx.info,n.name,t.title   FROM   cast_info AS ci, info_type AS it1, info_type AS it2, keyword AS k, movie_info AS mi, movie_info_idx AS mi_idx, movie_keyword AS mk, name AS n, title AS t  WHERE ci.movie_id = mi.movie_id AND ci.movie_id = mi_idx.movie_id AND ci.movie_id = mk.movie_id AND it1.id = mi.info_type_id AND it2.id = mi_idx.info_type_id AND k.id = mk.keyword_id AND mi.movie_id = mi_idx.movie_id AND mi.movie_id = mk.movie_id AND mi_idx.movie_id = mk.movie_id AND n.id = ci.person_id AND t.id = ci.movie_id AND t.id = mi.movie_id AND t.id = mi_idx.movie_id AND t.id = mk.movie_id AND ((it1.info)::text = 'countries'::text) AND ((it2.info)::text = 'rating'::text) AND ((mi.info)::text = 'USA'::text) AND ((n.gender)::text = 'm'::text);
q3#####SELECT n.name,t.title   FROM   cast_info AS ci, char_name AS chn, comp_cast_type AS cct1, comp_cast_type AS cct2, complete_cast AS cc, keyword AS k, kind_type AS kt, movie_keyword AS mk, name AS n, title AS t  WHERE cct1.id = cc.subject_id AND cct2.id = cc.status_id AND chn.id = ci.person_role_id AND ci.movie_id = cc.movie_id AND k.id = mk.keyword_id AND kt.id = t.kind_id AND mk.movie_id = cc.movie_id AND mk.movie_id = ci.movie_id AND n.id = ci.person_id AND t.id = cc.movie_id AND t.id = ci.movie_id AND t.id = mk.movie_id AND ((cct1.kind)::text = 'cast'::text) AND ((cct2.kind)::text ~~ '%%'::text) AND ((k.keyword)::text = ANY ('{neglect,unhappiness,illegitimate-son,ignoring-telephone,black-and-white,bitten-in-the-face,10,000-b.c.,knocked-out-with-gun-butt,absorbing-power,sleeping-with-a-light-on}'::text[])) AND ((kt.kind)::text = 'episode'::text) AND (chn.name IS NOT NULL) AND (((chn.name)::text ~~ '%man%'::text) OR ((chn.name)::text ~~ '%Man%'::text)) AND (t.production_year > 1996);

q998#####SELECT cn1.name,cn2.name,mi_idx1.info,mi_idx2.info,t1.title,t2.title   FROM   company_name AS cn1, company_name AS cn2, info_type AS it1, info_type AS it2, kind_type AS kt1, kind_type AS kt2, link_type AS lt, movie_companies AS mc1, movie_companies AS mc2, movie_info_idx AS mi_idx1, movie_info_idx AS mi_idx2, movie_link AS ml, title AS t1, title AS t2  WHERE cn1.id = mc1.company_id AND cn2.id = mc2.company_id AND it1.id = mi_idx1.info_type_id AND it2.id = mi_idx2.info_type_id AND kt1.id = t1.kind_id AND kt2.id = t2.kind_id AND lt.id = ml.link_type_id AND mi_idx1.movie_id = mc1.movie_id AND mi_idx2.movie_id = mc2.movie_id AND ml.linked_movie_id = mc2.movie_id AND ml.linked_movie_id = mi_idx2.movie_id AND ml.movie_id = mc1.movie_id AND ml.movie_id = mi_idx1.movie_id AND t1.id = mc1.movie_id AND t1.id = mi_idx1.movie_id AND t1.id = ml.movie_id AND t2.id = mc2.movie_id AND t2.id = mi_idx2.movie_id AND t2.id = ml.linked_movie_id AND ((cn1.country_code)::text = '[us]'::text) AND ((it1.info)::text = 'votes distribution'::text) AND ((it2.info)::text = 'votes distribution'::text) AND ((kt1.kind)::text = ANY ('{movie,tv series,tv movie,episode}'::text[])) AND ((kt2.kind)::text = ANY ('{movie,tv series,tv movie,episode}'::text[])) AND ((lt.link)::text ~~ '%eren%'::text) AND ((mi_idx2.info)::text < '9'::text) AND (t2.production_year = 2010);
q999#####SELECT mi.info,mi_idx.info,n.name,t.title   FROM   cast_info AS ci, info_type AS it1, info_type AS it2, keyword AS k, movie_info AS mi, movie_info_idx AS mi_idx, movie_keyword AS mk, name AS n, title AS t  WHERE ci.movie_id = mi.movie_id AND ci.movie_id = mi_idx.movie_id AND ci.movie_id = mk.movie_id AND it1.id = mi.info_type_id AND it2.id = mi_idx.info_type_id AND k.id = mk.keyword_id AND mi.movie_id = mi_idx.movie_id AND mi.movie_id = mk.movie_id AND mi_idx.movie_id = mk.movie_id AND n.id = ci.person_id AND t.id = ci.movie_id AND t.id = mi.movie_id AND t.id = mi_idx.movie_id AND t.id = mk.movie_id AND ((it1.info)::text = 'LD language'::text) AND ((it2.info)::text = 'top 250 rank'::text) AND ((mi.info)::text = 'English'::text) AND ((n.gender)::text = 'f'::text);
